 iske alaava ye bhi tha ki unke congress virodh ne, wo bhi is kathorta se ki na vyaktitv kaa khyaal, na sabhyataa kaa, na shishtataa kaa, janata main ek prakaar kii bechaini paidaa kar di

 hinduon main josh paidaa karnaa va unki raksha ke prabandh karne ke liye aavashwayak na tha ki zehar faile

 kya aaj ke din 84 or 2002 ke dangon ke prati sabhi ko praayshchit nahin karnaa chahie tha

 unhone tab aresas par pratibandh lagaaya

 Apart from this, it was also that his Congress opposition, that too with the strictness that neither the care of personality, nor of civilization, nor of civility, created a kind of uneasiness in the public
 inke saare bhaashan sampradayik vish se bhare the

 is zehar kaa fal ant main yahi hua ki gandhi ji kii amuly jaan kii qurbaani desh ko sahani padi
 The entire sympathy of the government and people was not with the RSS, but against them
 gandhi ji kii mrityu par aresas waalon ne jo harsh prakat kiya or mithai banti, usase yah virodh or bhi bad gaya
 In these circumstances, there was no other way for the government to take steps against the RSS
 is pratimaa ko lekar sardaar sarovar baandh ke aas paas ke gaanv ke logon ne sawaal uthaae hai
 People from 72 villages said that they would observe a fast in protest against the unveiling of the statue on 31 October
 chulhaa band rahegaa

 ham inhen ke aasare jite rahe hai, lekin ab sab nasht kiya ja rahaa he

 praudh logon ko 60 rupee kaa tikat lagegaa or bacchon ko 60 rupee

 tajmahal se 20 karod kii kamai hoti he

 kahin sardaar ko bada kiya ja rahaa he to kahin indira ko

 isse hamaare raajnneeti badi banati na ki choti ho jaati

 in tasveeron main aap rahul gandhi or sonia gandhi ke alaava anya congressi netaaon ko dekh rahe hai

 congress par aarope lagata he ki usne patel kii viraasat ko kabhi aage nahin kiya

 unki janmashati par bharat ke is mahaan sapoot ko salaam karata hum

 He then banned the RSS

 On 11 September 1948, he wrote a letter to Patel's RSS sarsanghchalak MS Golwalkar that it is one thing to organize and help Hindus, but to take revenge on the helpless and innocent men, women and children for their suffering is another matter
 iske alaava ye bhi tha ki unke congress virodh ne, wo bhi is kathorta se ki na vyaktitv kaa khyaal, na sabhyataa kaa, na shishtataa kaa, janata main ek prakaar kii bechaini paidaa kar di

 We have been living around them, but now everything is being destroyed
 kya aapako nahin lagata ki yah kisi kii maut par jashn ke samaan he

 tourist spot ban gaya he

 agar aap Observation Deck view, nahin janaa chahenge to uske liye alag se package he
 Adult people will get 60 rupees tickets and children 60 rupees

 BJP leader Smriti Irani is as much discussed in the Amethi seat of UP as in the 2019 Lok Sabha elections
 yah seat congress kaa garh rahi he or is seat se congress adhyaksh rahul gandhi(rahul Gandhi) ke khilaaf smriti irani chunaav lard rahi hai
 The BJP has played this stance only to contest Rahul as Smriti gave a tough fight in the 2014 Lok Sabha elections too
 amethi ko shuruyaat se hi gandhi parivaar ke prabhaav vaali seat mana jaataa he lekin is baar bijepi puri koshish kar rahi he ki vah is seat par apana kuch prabhaav jamaa sake isliye usne jujharu netaa kii chhavi vaali smriti irani ko chunaav main khadaa kiya he
 However, in the 2014 Lok Sabha elections, Smriti lost to Rahul by nearly one lakh votes
 isse pehle 2004 main smriti irani congress ke senior netaa kapil sibbal ke khilaaf dilli ke chandani chowk se chunaav lard chuki hai
 Smriti was born on 23 March 1976 in Delhi
 unke pita punjabi or maa bengali thim
 Smriti was the eldest of three sisters, so she started working when she was in the tenth class
 ek beauty product ke pramotion ke liye unhen ek din ke 200 rupye milte the
 Smriti first came into the limelight when she participated in the Miss India competition, which was held in 1998
 haalanki vah isamen safal nahin ho pain lekin isse unhen pahchaan jarur mili
 Smriti then moved to Mumbai where she initially worked at mcdonald's to earn money
 2001 main vah parsi vyapaaree jubin irani ke saath shaadi ke bandhan main bandha gayi
 Irani's professional life changed when she got Ekta Kapoor's serial
 is serial kaa naam tha 'kyonki saas bhi kabhi bahu thi
 In this serial, Smriti played the role of Tulsi, which became very popular in every household
 is serial ne smriti ko khub pahchaan dilaai
 In 2003, she left acting and joined politics
 ab unhen raajnneeti main aae hue kareeb dedh dashak biit chukaa he
 In 2004, she became the vice president of the youth wing of BJP Maharashtra
 2004 main hi unhone dilli ke chandani chowk se congress ke senior netaa kapil sibbal ke khilaaf chunaav ladaa
 Although she lost this election
 phir unhen bijepi kii kendriya samiti kaa agxcutive member banaaya gaya or 2010 main vah party kii rashtriya sachiv or mahila wing kii adhyaksh banaai gayi
 In 2011, Smriti was made a member of the Rajya Sabha
 2014 ke loksabhaa chunaavon main unke naam kii charchaa isliye bhi tej ho gai kyonki unhone amethi main rahul gandhi ke khilaaf loksabhaa chunaav ladaa
 During this time she gave a tough fight to Rahul but she lost by one lakh votes
 rahul ke khilaaf chunaav haarane ke baavjood 2014 main unhen centre main maanav sansaadhan vikaas mantralay diya gaya, haalanki baad main unhen kendriya kapadaa mantri banaaya gaya
 In the 2019 Lok Sabha elections, she is once again giving a tough fight to Congress President Rahul Gandhi in Amethi
 chuttee se lautne ke baad modi sarkaar ko har morche par gherne kii koshish kar rahecongress upaadhyaksh rahul gandhiko ab apane sansadeey kshetra kii bhi yaad aane lagi he

 agar jetali rajyasabha yaa rajyon main vidhaan parishadon kii samaapti ko lekar bahes hi karnaa chaahate hai, kisi faisle par pahunchnaa chaahate hai to samvidhan sabha kii bahes se unhen kaaphi kuch sahaara mil saktaa he, lekin unhen bataanaa to chahie ki jis rajyasabha main ve khud kai kanoonon kaa virodh karte rahe hai usee sadan main unke kanoon kaa virodh hone par dhiraj kyon jawaab de rahaa he
 The Rajya Sabha is the representative body of the states
 mantriparishad rajyasabha ke prati zimmedaar nahin hota he
 If the government does not have a majority in the Rajya Sabha, then the control of the house becomes certain over the government
 aisa prathit hota he ki arun jetali ko yahi mahasoos ho rahaa he
 Nevertheless, there are enough provisions that if there is a conflict in both the houses then a joint session can be called
 aisa teen baar ho chukaa he, lekin samvidhan main kahin nahin likhaa he ki yah das baar nahin ho saktaa he
 Now come to the debate in the Constituent Assembly on the Second Chamber ie Rajya Sabha or Legislative Council
 par ek saavdhaanee baratiyegaa
 Often, leaders cite disagreement and consensus in the Constituent Assembly debate
 bahes ke dauraan jataai gai asahmati ko aap faisle ke upar nahin rakh sakate kyonki wo faisla matdaan yaa sarvasammati se hua hota he
 Many politicians do this, but the responsible citizen should not
 6 janvari 1949 bhi guuruuvaar kaa din tha or 13 may 2015 bhi guuruuvaar jab arun jetali ne rajyasabha ke vivekadhikaar par sawaal uthaae
 In the world of Internet, there is a lot of inquiries about such coincidences, hence it is written otherwise it has nothing to do with the debate
 samvidhan sabha ke saamne sawaal tha ki kya rajyon main vidhaan parishad honi chahie
 Renuka Ray of West Bengal was against the Legislative Council and the concept of a double house
 unka kahana tha ki agar ucch sadan ko yahi pareekshan karnaa he ki kanoon jaldbaazi main to nahin bana he to iske liye rajyapal or raashtrapati ko paryaapt adhikaar he ki ve sadan se bill par dobaaraa vichaar karne ke liye aagrah kar sakate hai
 The pace of legislating from the second house will slow down, while India needs to make laws faster in the economic and social sphere
 isliye hamen abhi hi tay kar lenaa chahie ki samvidhan main duusare sadan kii vyavastha hi na ho
 There is no benefit from it
 ek or sadsy o ve alagesan virodh karte hue kehete hai ki sardaar vallabh bhai patel ne bhi prantiy samvidhan cameti kii report pesh karte hue kaha he ki ek hi sadan hona chahie
 i believe it is nothing but old age pension for leaders
 ajeeb sanyog he jo raay 1949 main thi vahi raay aaj bhi sunne ko mil jaati he
 Rajya Sabha is the retiree only
 lekin ham kaise maan len ki arun jetali ritair rajaneta he, jo pension ke liye vahaan hai ! In response to this debate, Dr
 BR Ambedkar says that i have no firm opinion in favor of the Second Chamber
 kai maamalon main yah behatar bhi ho saktaa he
 This debate has been going on since the time of the Constituent Assembly of France
 ambedkar kisi abe saiye ke ek kathan kaa hawala dete hai ki agar ucch sadan nimna sadan( loksabhaa) se sahamat ho jaae to yah vyarth hi he lekin agar sahamat na ho to bekaar hi he
 You readers must have understood this pinch
 lekin doctor ambedkar kehete hai ki french samvidhan sabha ne is raay ko kabhi sweekaar nahin kiya
 There is also a Second Chamber
 yah zarur he ki samvidhan main second chember kii vyavastha to he magar prayog ke taur he
 That is why we have not considered the Second Chamber permanent in the draft Constitution
 ise samaapt karne kaa praavdhaan bhi diya he
 As of now, it should be accepted in the Constitution as an agreement
 tippaniyan If we make haste to mention the debates of the Constituent Assembly from here, then we should consider why the role of Rajya Sabha was questioned
 loksabhaa main bhi kai sarkaron ne bina bahumat ke kaam kiya he
 The cries of not having a majority have also cried, but no one has said that the majority of the people who are in government should question the discretion of the House only occasionally
 satr dar satr nahin karnaa chahie
 Where is it written that the discretion of the Lok Sabha is final or should be
 kanoon ko lekar nyaaypalika se bhi to takaraav ho saktaa he
 After the election, the public will leave their discretion in the Lok Sabha
 yah saaf nahin he ki jetali rajyasabha kaa moolyankan kis tarah se karte hai
 Do they want a majority monopoly or are they advocating not giving space to disagreements
